## Instruction

Help me automatically update the two existing tables in the PURCHASE_INVOICE database with all the received receipts in my workspace. For receipts that are not fully paid, send an email to the relevant purchasing manager with the subject "Process Outstanding Invoices". The email body should include all the filenames that the manager still needs to process. Also, set a column description for outstanding_flag precisely as: "0=Paid, 1=Outstanding".

## Initial State

### Database

The database is rebuilt on each test; you can review the data construction process [here](https://github.com/hkust-nlp/mcpbench_dev/tree/finalpool_dev/tasks/finalpool/payable-invoice-checker/preprocess).

<Expandable title="Details">
```json arguments
{
	"query": "\nSELECT \n    i.PURCHASER_EMAIL,
	\n    i.INVOICE_ID,
	\n    i.SUPPLIER_NAME,
	\n    i.INVOICE_AMOUNT,
	\n    p.PAYMENT_AMOUNT,
	\n    (i.INVOICE_AMOUNT - p.PAYMENT_AMOUNT) AS OUTSTANDING_AMOUNT\nFROM PURCHASE_INVOICE.PUBLIC.INVOICES i\nJOIN PURCHASE_INVOICE.PUBLIC.INVOICE_PAYMENTS p ON i.INVOICE_ID = p.INVOICE_ID\nWHERE p.OUTSTANDING_FLAG = 1\nORDER BY i.PURCHASER_EMAIL,
	 i.INVOICE_ID\n"
}

```

```json arguments
{
	"query": "\nSELECT \n    i.INVOICE_ID,
	\n    i.SUPPLIER_NAME,
	\n    i.INVOICE_AMOUNT,
	\n    i.PURCHASER_EMAIL,
	\n    i.INVOICE_DATE,
	\n    p.PAYMENT_AMOUNT,
	\n    p.OUTSTANDING_FLAG\nFROM PURCHASE_INVOICE.PUBLIC.INVOICES i\nJOIN PURCHASE_INVOICE.PUBLIC.INVOICE_PAYMENTS p ON i.INVOICE_ID = p.INVOICE_ID\nWHERE i.INVOICE_ID LIKE '2024-%' OR i.INVOICE_ID LIKE 'BL-2024-%' OR i.INVOICE_ID LIKE 'INV-2024-%' \n   OR i.INVOICE_ID LIKE 'MCP-%' OR i.INVOICE_ID LIKE 'PO%24'\nORDER BY i.INVOICE_DATE DESC\n"
}
```

```json arguments
{
```
```json arguments
	"query": "SELECT i.INVOICE_ID,
	 i.SUPPLIER_NAME,
```

<Expandable title="Details">
```json arguments
{
	"query": "SELECT \n    COUNT(*) as total_invoices,
	\n    SUM(CASE WHEN p.OUTSTANDING_FLAG = 1 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as outstanding_invoices,
	\n    SUM(CASE WHEN p.OUTSTANDING_FLAG = 0 THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) as paid_invoices\nFROM PURCHASE_INVOICE.PUBLIC.INVOICES i\nJOIN PURCHASE_INVOICE.PUBLIC.INVOICE_PAYMENTS p ON i.INVOICE_ID = p.INVOICE_ID"
}

```

```json output_result
  PAID_INVOICES: 1007
```
